et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and the pain leaps out, just as we have said about the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work, there is fear that the patient may die immediately, or an ulcer may occur which cannot be healed.
de la mice	about the mouse
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of the mouse in the ways we have mentioned for the treatments, and it does not help, then there are three types of cautery that are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	and one method is that you make three cauteries, or four, along the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the liver cautery that we have said before;
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand over the entire cautery, and let the patient lie on their back;
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	and another method of cautery is that you heat the cautery which has two prongs, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and lift the area where the mouse is located, or where the side of the patient turns towards the left, and let the elevations by which you lift the area be according to the curvature, according to the length of the body, and the cautery should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After you put the two burning nerves until the heart is pierced from the other side, and then pull out the cautery, and thus there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you wish, then cauterize the entire cautery to three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has discharged pus for a long time, and this is better than the other treatments previously mentioned.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cautery is not useful for a dropsical person, except in the manner which is called "asclytes.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat it according to the methods we have said in divisions, and your treatment does not help, then you must make four cauteries around the boil, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one on the spleen, and two behind the back on the spine, and one at the armpit.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cautery be close to the surface of the heart.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After leave the cautery open to expel pus for a long time, and do not neglect the patient’s treatment after the cautery;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing would be hastened, and the two intents will be together with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cautery for the belly is the key that we have shown before;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and the one for the back should be olive-shaped, according to what is set forth above.
de l’enfleure des piez	about the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in one who is dropsical, and are full of yellow water, you must cautery on the back of the foot between the little toe and the ring toe;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and lift your hand with the cautery without turning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply with the point, so as not to break through the yellow bile, and let the cauterization be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After make on both legs two cauteries on each leg at the point of the kneecap;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the cauteries be long, one below the knee in front and the other outside, midway on the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauteries open for a long time without cleaning, so that the pus may come out;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after cleansing with the other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When the discharge from the stomach comes from cold and moisture, such that the retentive and digestive virtues which are in the stomach and intestines are weakened, and cannot be cured by means of treatments;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient well suffering and of great virtue, then make a large cautery on the stomach according to what has been spoken here before about the stomach cautery, the circular cautery;
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and four subtle cauteries around the buttock to every subtle claw cautery, and two cauteries on the thighs.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moistures abundant and the patient suffering, make a cautery on the wrist, and a cautery on each thigh, and two small cauterizations on the stomach near the large one, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the hemorrhoids are in the anus, one or more, and are old and consist of large cold and moist corrupted humors, and are treated as we have said in the sections, and it does not help, then make cauteries:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	three on the spine of the back, those which are completely outside under the almandate, little by little in a triangular shape, and one cautery under the buttock two fingers;
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think that his stomach is cooled, and the meat does not cook, and swelling of the face is seen, then on the face one makes a large cautery on the stomach, as was said before, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen with the entire key-shaped cautery;
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and leave the cautery open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treating the place until it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the fleshiness which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cauterize an abscess, heat the cautery that resembles a shaver, and then place it fully ablaze on the cut abscess;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and keep your hand there until the cautery reaches the origin of the vein, from which the blood flows;
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is much abscess, then cauterize each one as we have said;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the treatment of beneficial ointments until they are healed;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large cautery on the alcatia, it will have greater help.
de plaie mal curee	of a wound poorly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure surgery or incision, which we will discuss in its place, then such a disease comes that cannot be healed except by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When an ulcer comes to anyone, and it is old and discharges pus and corrupted moisture, then you should probe it thoroughly with a fine tent, and be sure to know the depth of the entire tent.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After heat the cautery that resembles a razor, and insert it into the fistula according to the amount of tent that has entered, and continue the cautery until the corrupted and putrid flesh is burned, once, or twice or thrice, according to the quantity needed;
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and beware of burning the nerves that are inside, and the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistula goes to the bladder and the intestine, then beware of these areas, and do not perform this outside the fleshy part, and consider that it is not penetrable;
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after care the wound until it is healed, and if the wound is cauterized, and the materials are removed for a long time, then know that the wound is entirely healed;
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the materials are not removed, know that the wound is deep, and the bone is corrupted at the root;
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus as one of those we will mention in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When cold pain comes to the testicles, and from great windiness, and he shows no interest in women, then you must make a cautery on the testicles on one side and the other with the key cautery that we have mentioned before;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauters in a line, and they will provide greater aid.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, so that the patient holds urine, then make a cautery on the outer part above the bladder, where the hairs of the groin begin, both to the right and to the left, and let each cautery be as long as the width of one thumb;
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and make a cautery on the back if you need to do so;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let the cauteries be made according to the form previously stated.
de la marris	of the marrow
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the matrix is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their periods are delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, she feels great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is necessary to make three cauterizations around the boil, as we have said in the cautery of the bladder, and two cauterizations outside the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let the cauteries be like a claw, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the viscous moisture descends into the hip joint, and for this reason it moves from its place, the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and the site of the departure is found near the joint, then you should cauterize the patient on the hip joint with a cautery resembling a circle, and mark in front of the site around the joint as it turns, so that the joint is inside the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and so let the cautery be such as those with which one has cauterized the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	and if this cautery is not available to you, make three large cauteries from olive oil, and let the cautery be as perfect as all the others;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the hip joint, and it is from cold and moisture, and the patient is treated with what we have said in the division and the treatment does not work, and the disease is old:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then you must purge the patient of thick humors with foul pills, or other good similar pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After you make cauterization;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the method of the cauterization is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	that is to know together burning medicines, and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cauterization is according to many methods, of which one is as follows:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the hip joint three triangular cauterizations according to this form, and make good depth and large, and have between each cauterization the space of a thumb's width, and let the cauterizations be olive-shaped;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	sometimes one makes a cauterization in the middle on top of the head of the hip, which is why there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you wish, then cauterize it with the circular cautery that we have mentioned before in the dislocation of the hip;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but do it in such a way that the circle contains the entire hip, and all the thickness of the thigh be burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the method used for sciatica, when the pain remains in the hip, and does not reach the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it extends to the thigh and the leg, make two cauteries there where the patient says the pain holds them, and one cautery above the ankle four times, on the left side a bit;
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cautery be knife-shaped, and let the thickness of the thigh be burned;
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain extends to the toes of the foot or nearby, cauterize where they feel the pain three times or four with the cautery which is called "point.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if necessary, do more to him;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if he feels that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, make a cautery with a knife or circular cautery, and be careful in all your cauterizations that you do not leave the cautery so long that you burn the nerves and large arteries, and that you do not cause more harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And myself I have seen many who made a cautery on the ankle of the foot, and left it so long that the leg was entirely swollen, and the foot also, and all the foot became pierced and corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a purgative from which he got death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, make a cautery in one and in the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise ones say about the cautery of the hip, here is the method: make such an iron and let it be at the head as thick as a date stone, or a little less, and let it be in sections and let there be between each section the space of a finger's breadth;
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let the splints be covered with two layers, and also let them be like knots, and there should be one well-made iron strap;
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	and let it be heated until it is all red and emits sparks, and then place it on the hip joint of the sick side, and turn it towards the healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and cauterize it once with one cautery and leave it for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then make a poultice of butter, and leave the wound open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment of anointing until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasis says that we use little of this cautery due to the fear of its gaze, and we see few who use it;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and nevertheless this is of the good cauterizations, which he can endure, and where it applies.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cautery of burning medicine is that you make the instrument to interweave in which descends the margin of the door, and it should be of bronze or iron with one side long, and in the height have two inches, and between each have the quantity of the thickness of a thumb;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and they should be open below and above, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After place on the hip box of the patient lying on his healthy side, and press your hand much on the hip box;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After put between the two circles of the hot awl which is heated by fire one pouce, and leave it for one hour of time, and let the patient bear the heat and the dryness of it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For there he finds a burning as if from fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the burning has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the hip with a gentle awl, and leave it this way for three days, and apply butter until what is black from the scalding is removed;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and leave it for three days so that putrefaction may come out;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the final aid after the treatment of ointments until he is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or to the leg, make an instrument that adheres well according to what you have done on the hip equally;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the method of hot water, and I have written it in the treatise on the rectification of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and vitriol, an equal amount of each, and grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	where there is a small opening to allow the blade of a razor to enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and put on top of that pot another well-sealed pot, and add alkali and heat and sweet water on top, until there is two fingers above the powders when you have well pressed it in your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and let it be thus until the liquid drips down and falls into a pot, then take all that liquid and throw it onto hot coals and onto alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then it will be very liquid and is administered in many works of medicine and in cauterizations of other parts.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it performs work like fire, and there are other medicines with which one cauterizes the hip well, such as resin and honey anacardium and heat with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galien tells us of a treatment where a man was cured of the pain in his hip and sciatic nerve, and he praises it greatly, and says that no other treatment was done, and that he was healed all at once when this treatment was performed, and he bathed as it is taught hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And he says that you should take fresh and dry green litharge, and grind it well with a little fat, and apply it to the hip and thigh and leg where the pain is, and leave it;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leave for three hours by the quantity that the patient no longer feels the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make him enter the bath until his body is a bit warmed, and make him enter the bed, and the pain will completely go away and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use fire cautery of such medicines, if it is not after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's fat, it helps greatly;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cautery should be done in such a manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take wool and anoint it with old oil, and place it on the groove that is between the big toe and the other one which is called the instep.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After take dry goat's fat, and apply it to fire until it is charcoal, and put it on the wool, and leave it until it melts;
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and do again in this way, and do not stop doing so until you think by feeling that it reaches to the hip, and the pain ceases;
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this kind of cautery is called "goat cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by falling or from percussion or from too great an evacuation, or from similar cold matter spread out, none of these appearances is suitable for cauterization, because it comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary after the patient has been emptied of foul pills or other similar things, that one makes on his back, where the pain holds, three lines marked with ink, and in each line five cauteries or more according to the strength and quantity that the patient can endure;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and let the cautery be done according to the cautery which is called "point";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you wish, make three or four cauteries with the medium-sized clamp according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Often this disease comes to small children, and the signs of the beginning are that they have tight groins when they rise, and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you find at the back of the spine and in us the appearance which comes over the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and wish to treat it, then cauterize it with the circular cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cautery marks each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you wish, then cauterize around the spine with a sharp cautery two lines or three, and let the points be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treat the area until it is healed according to what we have said, and beware that you do not apply cautery to swelling that is in spasms of a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When the pain of joints is from moisture that has spread to each member of the body, and when pain comes in feet, which the physician properly calls "gout," and when it is of cold cause and treatments of medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cauterization in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	make many cauterizations around the joint of the foot, and let the cauterizations be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is need that you press on the sole of the foot, then make a cautery across the entire point called "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come down to the knees and other joints, and this often happens, then make cauterizations on each knee three or four in each part, with the entire cauterization being olive-shaped;
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	and if you have need of more, then make more, but do not hold your hand out any longer than it takes for the point of the heart to be burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend as far as the knees and to the back, then the administrator should apply the cautery that we have mentioned in our chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	and if the pains are in the hands, then make points around the elbow two inches;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there remains any pain in the fingers, then make points on each joint and on the palm of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pains come down to the ribs or up to the shoulders, then cauterize each part, and give good care to the patient and prepare medications.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give him good care and you purge phlegm, he will be healed by the grace of God.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the rupture of the spleen
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When rupture comes in the groin, and the bowel descends to the testicles and this is newly occurred, then it is necessary that when you wish to treat it, he should not eat on that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and he uses things that loosen the belly, so that the bile descends from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after he makes him sit on his back between your hands, and commands him to stretch his wrist until the veins appear, and you hold them with your fingers, and stretch downward from the joint above the bone of the wrist, and make a sign that resembles half a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then heat the cautery of which this is the form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	until it becomes white and gives off sparks.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	then return the veins to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the minister stretches his hand so they do not retreat back;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and work well on the thighs of the patient, and put a cushion under him and a bolster on the thighs, and another on the part that holds the hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then put the cautery on the mark with your whole hand, and hold it straight and keep it until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, then repeat again until you come to the bone;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and be careful that the blister does not burst when you make the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	that you do not burn it too much;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that by this the patient does not die, or suffer other harms.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cauterization of children be subtle according to the measure of eggs, and for large people likewise as big according to their measure;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	After three days, treat the area of the cauterization with butter until the scalding is removed;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after treating with other ointments until it is healed, and the patient lies forty days on his back until the wound is well sealed;
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary that his nourishments be diluted for a long time, so that the scabs do not protrude when he begins to move around in rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise, let him be given a well-made bandage, and wear it for another forty days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and let him have good rest, that he labors little and guards against too great fullness of drink and food, and of too loud shouting;
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he follows this teaching, then is he entirely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say hereafter the treatment of cutting in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Of the rupture of the belly.
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ruptures occur in other parts of the body and are known, and you see that they do not grow larger, then make a cautery according to its size, and let a third of it be burned;
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	afterwards treat it according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and some of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with a three-cornered cautery according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but mark first the place to join and make a line across the width above the rupture, and another outside, and hold your hand right in the middle of the key-shaped cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cautery is lighter and more gentle.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes in any limb, whether from falling or striking, and that pain lasts a long time, and medical treatment does not help, then it should be cauterized with the cautery called "points," and the cautery should be according to the length of the limb and its smallness and weakness and virtue and location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if he is healed by the first cautery, it is good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	if that name, begin another cautery on that spot, for such is the custom that it must change to the part that is closest, therefore you must make the cauteries until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	of mixing
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The mixtures are sometimes aided by cautery with great help, and especially the diseases that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	When you see to cauterize, beware if the disease is in its beginning, and if it is treated according to what we have said in the division, and does not spread nor remain, and you fear that the corruption may spread throughout the patient, then make five cauteries on the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	one in the middle of the head, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the hair;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and two on the two horns, and one behind on the nape;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and keep your hand there until the cauterization reaches the bone, and until the scabs come out so that the vapors from the thick humors can escape;
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize on the joint according to what is mentioned before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the miliaria is spread everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and if it is clearly present, then you should cauterize it with these cauteries that we have mentioned at the head, and one cauterization on top of the neck, and two cauteries on the spine of the neck, and six cauteries on the spine of the back, and one large one on the rump and another nearby, and two on the two shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and two on the ribs, and two on the tendons of the breast, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and beware of the nerves that are on the last heel, that you do not burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and sometimes one makes a cautery on the bone of the wrist, and another on the bone of the stomach, and another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that when I do more cauteries, I provide more help, and it benefits him;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	and know that the patient does not feel any pain from the cautery as the healthy person feels it, because the body is already entirely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauterizations be large and small according to the limbs and the joints, according to what you will find in methods of the irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, apply the place with flour of Veronica and honey and other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling comes to any limb and is treated with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healed, then make cauterizations on the limb according to the size and smallness of the limb;
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cauterization slightly penetrate into the thickness of the skin;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes cauterization is done to the hand and foot and back, at the nerve endings that move the limb, and thus the swelling is removed;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and in any case, no one should intervene if they are not knowledgeable about the limbs and the nerve endings that move the body.
de albaras	of arthritises
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease which is called «albaras» is awakened, and medical treatments are of no use, then cauterize it with a cautery a bit thoroughly, according to the quantity of the thickness of the tumor, until the swelling is removed, and its color changes;
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	then treat with flour of vetches and lentils with rose oil and leaves of plantain, and blood of pigeon and blood of lark, of each one part;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and mix everything together, and bind it with a cloth, and apply it to the place until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment of chancre by cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When chancre comes at the beginning, and you wish to stop it, then cauterize it with a cautery that resembles a circle, all around the edge of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And moreover, the wise say that one should also make a cautery in the middle of the ulcer;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and all the same this does not seem good to me, for I fear that it might become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already seen it happen at times;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and it is more advisable that it be cauterized around with the cautery which is called "circle", as we have said much about cauters.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has a disease which is called "adubelati", and it lingers in dying either due to the excess it causes or due to the age of the patient when they are decrepit (that is to say too old) and have little blood, or due to the season;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you wish to hasten its end:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then cauterize around with many small cauteries while pressing;
aprés le laisse ensi.	afterwards leave it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will hasten to moisturize.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you wish to pierce it with the entire cautery, then heat the cautery in this manner which is its form:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of that disease which is called "adubelati" until the cautery has pierced the heart, and let the cautery be such that the patient feels it externally in such a way that the course of the putrefaction is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment until he is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	the fire treatment by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of disease there is which is called "corrodens," and it is nothing other than a consumption of the limb, for it consumes the limbs as fire consumes dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a place that can withstand fire together with cautery, then heat the key-shaped cauteries both small and large, according to what is appropriate for the location where the disease is;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	afterwards cauterize all around until you reach all the corruption, and none of it remains, so that everything which is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and put on the cauterized places boiled wool with oil until the burns from the fire are removed, and all of the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After that, apply ointments that promote flesh growth.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that healthy flesh does not grow, it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if not, then repeat the cautery on what remains of the corrupted areas.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this mangling has sometimes been cured by medicine applied instead of fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but nevertheless fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already stated the treatment with medicine in the section:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the veins that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Very often, a disease called "clos" according to our understanding arises on the feet from the outside, and it is a large, inflamed thing that hurts the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterization for this disease is according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cauterization, and hot water cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery is such that you heat the cautery to the length of a goose feather, and it should be made of good iron in a size that can surround the nail on all sides, and that there are fine edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	afterward, place it completely hot on the nail, and turn your hand all around the nail until it reaches the root of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and leave it thus for three days until it begins to expel pus;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then make a poultice of wild mallows crushed with tar, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nail will fall out and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then clean the ointment area by greasing the flesh until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they turn inward on the body, and this often happens in hands and feet, then you must apply a cautery of hot water;
et est en teil maniere:	and it is done in such manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take a reed of boxwood or iron, or a goose quill, and place it on the nail and the wart, that is to say, corns or warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and put the cane on so that it wraps all around, then put a pot of warm water on it, and hold your hand well, and press your hand while turning so that the edge of the cane comes to the root of the nail, and can find the way deep down to the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient endure the bite of the hot water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it thus, and it will be uprooted entirely from its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	So do one after another until you strengthen all those that are in the body, then treat them with ointments that generate flesh.
li cure dou trembler	cure the trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When someone shivers from cold or nerves, or from a quartan fever or another, then you should make four cauteries or four on the spine of the back, one cauterization between each vertebra;
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	And for the cautery with a weight, and on the stomach with the olive-shaped cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	let it shake, and the health hastens from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of smelly pus-filled boils
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Sometimes there appear on the outer part of the body baths, or smelly pus-filled boils, which come from corrupted large materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	and it is necessary at first when they appear to make a cautery on each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a fine cautery of myrtle wood, with which the tip is held to the fire, or of a long root of aristolochia, or a lentil-shaped cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear, in this manner, and they cannot grow any further, but the excess from which they come is broken, and they are healed;
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Often there are great flows of blood from the artery that is cut in the wound that comes to the surface, or in the incision of an abscess, or in the cautery of the limb, and similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is a very difficult thing to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And whenever this happens to someone, you must quickly place your index finger on the wound of the vein and press very hard until the blood is calmed beneath your finger, and no drop comes out;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then put the olive oil cauterization tools of various sizes over the fire until they are all red;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Then apply the cautery, whether large or small according to the wound and the place where the artery is cut, and put the cautery on that vein where you hold your finger, and keep the cautery so long that the blood is restrained.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it jumps out when you lift your finger from the vein, and the cauterizer is extinguished, then quickly take another of the cauterizers that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not stop doing this one after the other until the blood is stopped;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and be careful not to burn the nerve that is nearby, and that no other harm comes to the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when blood flows from an artery, it cannot be easily stopped unless by one of the four methods we have mentioned:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	either by cautery, or by extraction when it is not treated, or by tight binding with thread, or by applying medications that have the power to stop blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and let it be tied and held firmly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will administer compression by tightly binding with cloths or placing burning substances on it, or other similar things, does not help if the pus is not.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and there is no doctor or medicine present, then he must put his index finger on the vein wound as we have said, and stretch well until it remains over the wound and over the vein;
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and he should not move it, but moisten it with cold water often, which should be very cold, until the blood is frozen, thickened, and congealed;
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make preparations in advance for what he may need of cauterization and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of treatments for wounds.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases in which fire cauterization or burning medicines are needed, and the indications and causes and the ingredients and forms of the cauterizations;
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I have placed this chapter from head to foot, and I will proceed in this chapter by the same method so that one finds more easily what one wants.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And before I begin this, it is necessary, dear son, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of cauteries, and for that reason greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter there are many times evacuations of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and treating wounds, and extracting arrows, and incising stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and from it comes death to many.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you that you do not undertake folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many kinds of people come to treatments.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	they come from those who hate themselves so much with their illness that they change easily because of the madness they find in their disease, and the greatness of its malice;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and of these one must have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And there are some who give their sense and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	wait, I am a surgeon";
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the disease is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not fitting that you consent to those who come to you with this manner, but place greater trust in your honor than in your desire, and do not open foolishly but wisely about that which you are certain, and from which you can gain praise;
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use prognosis and indication in the treatments of your patients to whom health is to be restored;
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and this will help you to acquire good reputation, and glory, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, May our Lord grant you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to breathe of the holy inspiration of his hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered this chapter by dividing it into sections, according to what is before in the chapter of cauterizations, that I have divided from head to foot, so that you may find more easily what you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	from the head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	and you know that this disease often comes to children at birth, and when it gives too strong a pull on the child's head;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and sometimes this comes from a hidden cause that is unknown.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease except in children, and in all those I have seen, death was swift;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and for that reason, it seems to me that I should not leave the work in such cases.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw a child whose head was filled with water, and the head swelled each day until it could no longer support it;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and so wet with moisture that it was dead, and this moisture is gathered under the bone on the saphenous vein, between the heart and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the work is such that if the moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscess is small, you should split down the middle of the head a wide cut;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and let it be as long as two fingers, until the moisture flows;
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and here is the form of the spatula:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is thicker, and the abscess is larger, make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	and if the moisture is under the bone, and the signs that you see are the openings at the top of the head from each side, and the fluid jumps out forcefully when you press it with your hand from inside, and this does not return to you:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	so you must split the head in three splits according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, extract all the moisture out.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	after extracting the cloths and powders, put wine and oil in them, and leave it this way until the fifth day;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then untie it, and treat the wound with tents and ointments, and continue to bind the head evenly, and give the patient dry meat with little moisture until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incision is to look where the swelling of the abscess is most prominent and where the fluid has gathered;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for sometimes it is in front;
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes behind;
aucune fois en destre;	sometimes on the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut then the abscess when it is open, and the filling of the pus, and slit it according to what you are able;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and beware that you do not cut the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and if a flow of blood comes, so that the patient dies from the loss of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of rheumatism
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When it happens to someone a disease which is called "catarrh" in the eyes or nose, and the illness is old, and the medical treatment does not help, then the final treatment is cauterization along with cutting the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is therefore necessary, when you cut the veins, that the patient tilt their head back;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	afterwards he rubs the area with a coarse cloth until the arteries appear, then the patient tightens his neck around the entire cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	then look where the vein is located, and the areas from one to the other are behind the ears, and they are positioned there;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	then mark the areas to incise, then cut one and the other with a sharp two-edged spatula until the cut reaches the bone, and this should be done across the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you wish, place the knife under the artery and cut above it, slicing also in two parts across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, the blood will spurt up continuously forcefully.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	and if the artery does not appear upon feeling, then you must measure the space of three fingers, then mark to incise and cut until the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and the amount of blood that should be let out is six ounces, and perhaps a little more or less, according to what the patient can bear, and the replenishment of the artery;
puis regarde la plaie:	then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if any of the abscess remains on the bone, cut it so that no hot abscess comes, then drain the wound and tie it up, and treat it with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an old migraine comes with a sharp catarrh, due to the moisture of tears and the heat in the temples and the old snot forcefully emerging and similar things, and it is treated by methods of medical treatments but all that does not help him, then we draw the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the method of extracting them is that the patient should pull back the hairs from their temples and pay attention to the artery that appears in the temple, for it shows well by its pulsation, and it is slightly set outward than in some men who are too cold;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is replaced, then the patient tightens its neck with some cloths, then rubs the area with a rough cloth, and rinses the area with warm water until the artery appears clearly;
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatula of which this is the form:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then lightly peel the skin until you reach the artery, then pull it up to the tweezers, and carefully separate the tissues that are beneath it on each side;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is delicate, then turn it with the tip of the hook, then cut it from that part according to the quantity of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, then the sinew does not jump entirely throughout.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	and draw blood from six ounces down to three;
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	and if the artery is large, then you must tie it in two places with a strong double thread of silk, so that corruption does not come before the healing of the wound, and bleeding occurs;
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	then cut off the excess that is between the two ties at the same hour, and then, if you wish, cauterize it with a knife cautery until the head is cut to the bone;
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and it is the most difficult work if the patient does not have fever and is of a hot temperament.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For cauterization is a help to finish the moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	for that reason, it is of greater help to the moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	For the extraction of arteries, it is necessary to fill the place with old cotton and put well-made bandages on top;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when they are untied, be careful with dry medicines that promote flesh growth and bandages until it is healed;
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	and if there is bleeding from the artery as long as you work on it, hasten to cut by cautery, or use verdigris in the place and press with your hand until the blood is stopped;
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you do not have that available, put your thumb on the place until the blood is congealed, and wash the place with cold water until the bleeding stops, and press as necessary;
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	and that which is better and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this sharp cautery of two parts, but let the blade be well thick to retain its heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instrument is too thin, it holds less of its heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	and there should be one inch of thickness between the two blades, and then when you have marked where to join the two places, and you place the burning iron until it reaches the bone, and cut the vein in two parts;
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and they should be separated between the two shoulders because it is not fully soldered with this cautery throughout;
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and this is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	and when the tears of the eyes are descending from the veins that are on top of the head due to fire, and medical treatment does not help, and you see the face of the patient redden, and feel a trembling on the forehead as if shaking;
