And if the abscess is of the kind of scrofula, then cut it as we have said for incisions of scrofula, and if the wound emits pus, then apply cauterization as we have said before.
de la routure de l’artere	of the rupture of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When the artery is cut, and the skin above is sewn, often abscesses result, and similarly it happens to swollen veins and abscesses;
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	and one knows it thus for the artery, the abscess is long in appearance;
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	and when you feel it with your hands, you sense the constriction;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	and when it is for the vein, it appears soft and more visible;
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	and it is foolish to cut this abscess, especially when it is under the ribs and in the angles and on the neck and in many other places, and it is very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	It is necessary then to avoid the iron treatment, and that which is at the head should also be avoided, and in that which is swollen from the artery make a cut above the skin of the long;
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	then work the size at the incisions, and carefully separate the artery from the tissues until it is exposed;
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	then place a needle underneath it and make it pierce to the other side, and tie the artery with a double thread in two places, according to what I have taught you in the extraction of the two arteries that are in the temples;
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	then puncture the area between the two ties with an introducer until the pus comes out that is there, and let the abscess be drained;
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	then administer the treatment that induces vomiting, until the bile flows;
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat it with an ointment suitable for this, until it is healed;
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	and if the abscess is the size of a vein, then you should stain your hand with what you can from the abscess to all the skin, then insert the needle under the area that you hold in your hand, and pierce it, and have double thread so that you pull it from the other side;
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	then tie the abscess, as I have said, with the thread of one of the two ends of the doubled thread;
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	and if you fear that the thread might come out, then insert another needle through the entire thread under the abscess at the incision of the first needle, and tie the threads in four places;
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	then cut the abscess until the excess flows out, then cut the excess of the heart and leave what is attached;
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then put on the wet cloth in wine and oil, then administer treatments of bandages and ointments until he is healed.
des apostemes des ners	of abscesses of the nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	As abscesses come in the artery and vein, so do abscesses come to the nerves when they are wounded, or by too much labor, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And this happens more often in the shoulders and hands and all joints, and it is a severe abscess, and its color resembles the color of the flesh, and it is in many positions without pain;
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	and when it is pressed firmly, the patient feels pain, and it is not part of the flesh, but beneath the heart;
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	and it moves well on all sides, and does not go forward or backward, nor below or above, and the one that is in the joints should not be cut with iron:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	by chance there might be contraction;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	and for those on the head or forehead, cut the skin with a spatula.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, hold it with tweezers, and cut it at its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it is large, suspend it with a lancet, scrape it, then remove it and suture the wound, and treat it until it heals.
des grosses boces pendans	large hanging boils
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Sometimes it happens in the abdomen and not elsewhere, and it is a disease called "fungus" due to its resemblance to mushrooms, and its roots are subtle, and the head is large;
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	and there are small and very large ones;
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	and I saw a man who had two in his belly that were more like fungi than anything else, and there was no difference, and they were white, and had a small root, and were deeply split, and moisture immediately flowed from them.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I cut them and found that one weighed eighteen ounces, and the other six and a half, and in the work of the incision you must observe if the patient is moist, and the color of the joint is white and moist and has a fine root;
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	so you cut it with a broad spatula, and have the fire cauterizer present.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For in cutting there often come too great outflows of blood, and if the blood overcomes you, then hasten to cauterize;
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	and if you see the patient is fainting and fearful of the iron incision, then take a well-made thread of linen, and bind the joint as we have said, and leave it for two days;
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	and then bind it, and do not stop straining the thread of linen until it cuts through the joint, and it falls off without effort;
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	and if the roots are large, there is fear in cutting, especially for the abdomen, but you can cut off half of it, then cauterize so that it does not return;
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	Then treat the wound, and be careful not to cut the tissue which is of reddish color and has poor sensation and looks like milk when examined.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is an abscess infected, and I will come to the treatment of the sore afterward.
quant li boude ist fuer	When the boil is about to burst.
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of the pus comes from the cautery of a wound or a split in the surface, and it is on the belly and some of the pus comes out, as it happens in other ruptures, or from blood that flows from veins or arteries according to what was mentioned before, or from flatulence;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if it is due to the rupture of the surface and the discharge of pus, then the color of the abscess resembles the color of the flesh, and it is a light matter without pain, and it discharges through various outlets.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is due to the discharge of the intestines, then it is more varied, and when one presses it with their fingers, it sinks in and then returns, and sometimes it becomes hard, and greatly enlarges at the entrance of the bath and from strenuous labor.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it is due to moisture, it is a light matter, and it discharges well when you press it with your hand, and it does not resist;
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	and if it is for blood, then the abscess opens with these signs being large and hard, and is fixed according to a quantity;
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	and if it is for wind, then it is soft to the touch, and the work is such that you look to see if the appearance is due to artery blood, or vein blood, or wind.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	And it is necessary that you leave the treatment.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear with it, as I have said in the chapter about abscesses, concerning the artery and the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	and if the appearance is due to the intestine or the bile, then you must instruct the patient to soak their shoulder, and lie stretched out straight, then apply a poultice all around the swelling;
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	then command them to lie still between your hands, then go around the area you have poulticed with all the spatula, then stretch half of the abscess above with the entire large needle;
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	then bind around it with a strong thread, or a cord of strong silk firmly, and let the knot of the binding be secure;
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	then apply half of the abscess extended over the binding, and put your index finger in it, and squeeze the interior;
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	if you find it caught in the binding, then untie it, and push the interior outward from the belly;
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	and if you find the boil, then take it with the lancet, and cut off the excess;
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	and if the artery or vein resists you, go around gently, then return to your work and take two needles, and insert two strong threads, and place the two needles around what you have done in a cross so that you pierce it;
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	then extract the abscess in four places above the needles, and if you see, remove the needles, and leave the area until it becomes pus-filled, and the dead flesh will fall off by itself;
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	when it is thin and rotten, then cut it out, and treat it as necessary, and the abscess will fall off as we have said;
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	and extract the blood or moisture that you find, then treat the area as necessary, and sew up the area.
dou chancre	of the ulcer
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have discussed in the division the similarities of ulcers, and how one should work with medications, and how one should avoid iron treatment;
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	and we speak of the ulcer appearing in the marrow, and great caution is needed in its treatment, and the ancients said that when ulcers are in a place where they can be scraped off like ulcers on mammary glands, and in the thigh, and in similar places, they should be completely removed when they first begin;
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	and when it is large and old, you must not approach it, for I can never heal any of them;
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	and no one ever heals from it before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And the work, when it is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, is that you purify the patient of black bile;
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	then make him sweat if there is evident excess, then prepare the patient in a good place to perform the work;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	then place your poultices on the ulcer, and cover it entirely with hair, and remove it from all sides without leaving anything;
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and let the blood flow freely, and mark well the place with your hand or some object, and if the continuous flow of blood prevents you from making an incision in the artery or vein, then cauterize until the bleeding is stopped;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat with other treatments until it is healed.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have said before in the division the types of dropsy, and in what manner the accumulation of water is formed, and the signs of each type, and the treatment performed by medicines, and that which is treated by iron:
si est eclites soulement;	it is swollen solely;
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	and one should not use iron in these two types:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	It is to know, tympanites and hyposarcia, for these are mortal things;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	then when you treat this kind of dropsy which is called "eclites" with medicines, and the treatment does not help, look if the patient is weak, or if they have another disease besides dropsy, such as fever and diarrhea and similar things;
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	do not use iron, for there is danger;
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	and if you see the patient is of strong vigor, and they have no other disease but only dropsy, and they are not too young nor too old, then you must proceed thus:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	lift the patient upright on your hands, and have the assistants press the abdomen to push the water to the lowest part of the body, then take the spatholite spine according to this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let it be cutting of two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	the tip, and nevertheless it should not be so penetrating that it can reach the intestine when inserted, and it should not injure;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	then look if the dropsy is spreading towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	then you must make three straight cuts below the tumor down to the wrist;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if the dropsy is due to liver disease, then your incision should be on the left side of the tumor three fingers wide;
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it is due to mucus, then it should be on the right, and it is not suitable for the patient to lie on the incision so that the excess fluids do not flow to the weak area;
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	then pierce all the skin with the instrument, and insert it, and lift your hand to spread the spatula between the skin and the surface as in flaying to the quantity of one inch or so around;
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	then pierce the surface until the spatula reaches the hollow place, which is where the water lies, then pull it out forcefully, and insert this instrument of which here is the form:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it resembles a thin silver chain, and it is made of bronze or light iron, and at the lower part, there is a small perforation;
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and on one side, three perforations;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two from the other side, and one from another;
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the shoulder is cut like a quill, and this is the form of the incision with which the scribes cut the quill:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top above is the alembic, so that when the instruments come to the water, they now rise up on the instrument;
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	empty then half or a third part, for if you empty more than is appropriate at that hour, perchance the patient may die from the resolution of his spirit from the wound, or he falls into a stupor, or he approaches death;
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but empty according to the quantity of its strength, and according to what the conditions of the patient's strength signify, and his pulses;
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then draw the instrument and hold the liquid, and it is held now for the plug that stops the opening which is on the surface, of which I have spoken, that you pierce according to this manner;
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then use the instrument again the other day, if you see the patient tolerating this, and draw a small amount of liquid;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do this for several days, and be careful not to remove so much that only a little liquid remains.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you doubt about the patient, and you leave a lot of liquid, then treat with burial earth or hot sand, and by sweating a lot or bathing in the sun, and dye from drinking;
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	and the treatment with drying medicines until it is healed, and cauterize on the stomach and on the liver and on the spleen after the extraction of the water, as I have said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	about the obstruction of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born who have no opening in the penis, or the opening is small, or it is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary to pierce it immediately with a very fine instrument throughout according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	then put a fine cloth on the wound, and bind it and keep it that way for three or four days, and when he wants to urinate, remove the cloth, let him urinate, and then put it back;
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	and perhaps none is needed, because the urine that comes out forcefully does not leave it closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	He whose opening is small is treated with the plug of lint, as we have said, so it will widen.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who do not have the opening in its proper place are defective, because some are born with the opening at the tip of the penis, which prevents them from urinating unless they lift their penis up;
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	and they cannot menstruate because the matter cannot reach the uterus, and it is a bad disease.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the manner of the work is that the patient lies often on his back, then stretch the head of the penis and cut it as the length of a feather, so that the opening falls in the middle, as it befits;
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	and be careful of the bleeding that often occurs, and if it happens, stop it with what stops blood, and treat the wound until he is healed.
des pustules de la verge	pustules of the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Often this albathe comes in the penis, and it is an ugly appearance of flesh;
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	and there are malignant and non-malignant [ones];
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	and you must take them with a subtle knife, cut and clean them all, then put on moist cotton with Egyptian ointment;
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with diafinicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the abscess is malignant, of putrid color and stinking, then you must apply cauterization to it.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have cut it, and if the ulcer is at the tip of the penis, with part inside the skin and part outside, then you must remove the part of the ulcer that is inside first;
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	and when it is sealed, then treat the part outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For when you treat it all at once, the head of the penis is not secure and may be pierced, leading to blackening and corruption in the penis and the testicles;
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	so it is necessary to scrape off all that is black and corrupted, then apply the plaster of honey and flour which is made from pomegranate peel and vetches, then treat with other treatments until he is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if bleeding occurs, then apply the lunar cauterization according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cautery thus helps in two disposals together:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	that is, to the discharge of blood, and to corruption;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	and if the head of the penis is corrupted and retracted, then you must insert a cane of polnt into the urethra of the penis, and let the patient urinate through it;
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	and when the skin is swollen at the head of the penis which happens to those who have not been circumcised, or it happens due to a wound or an abscess, then you must peel it with a sharp instrument until the tissues are loosened, and the head of the penis is freed on all sides;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	and if it is a difficult thing to discuss this, then you must scrape with the spatula a little bit from the head of the penis and the skin;
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	then gently separate them between two, and place a thin linen cloth moistened with cold water, so it does not dry out again.
de la circoncision	of the circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not a separation of continuity like other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	nevertheless, when we perform this act of our will, and especially on children, it is necessary that we do the best work, and the least harmful to their well-being.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not practice circumcision on their children, for it is not used in their law, and we have nothing more than what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have seen the majority of masters and surgeons who performed circumcisions around the edge, with force, and with an entire novacule;
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	so flee the cuts because there are two layers, and by chance one might cut the top one and leave the bottom one.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	or the recovery is worse, and the pain is doubled, and in the cleaning which is of the wound, the tip of the member is not securely treated;
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	and in the cleaning of the nail, by chance the iron might slip, and ruin the work, and many times they grow back without needing cleaning, and I have wanted it so.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the cleaning that is done with force on all the thread of the ligament I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the force cuts exactly as well above as below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, you cut evenly in one continuous motion;
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but that the thread be tight around the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and the manner of the first work is that you make the child think, if he understands, that you do not do him harm by tying the thread around the penis only, and then give him hope in every way that you can;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	then make him stand between your hands straight, and respond to the forces between your hands or under your feet that the child does not see them, nor any of the instruments;
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	then put your hand on the penis and blow on the groin, and pull it up until the head of the penis is inside;
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	then clean it well of the filth that has gathered, then tie the marked place with a double thread, then tie it under one point to another tie;
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it with two hands by the second ligature at the pouch and index finger, and cut between the two ligaments, then quickly lift the heart up and pull the head of the rod;
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then let the blood flow little by little, for it is the medicine;
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and put powder on and on the powder, one cloth glued with a mixture of an egg white dissolved in rose water, cooked with good and fresh rose oil, and leave it on until the next day, and cure it again as needed until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form for the forces in purification is as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	the two shoulders should be held tight and be sharp, and the shoulders should be as large as the sleeve evenly:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The error of the purification is when the pus inside flows at the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	then it is necessary that you extend it with your nail, so that the area forms an abscess;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	and cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your nail, then hold it with forceps, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if it passes three days, and what is under the penis is swollen, then leave it until the heated abscess is calmed, and lightly scrape it;
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	then cut it as much as you can move it, and be careful of the part of the penis, for this will not harm it.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Treat then the area of things with a powder that we have mentioned in the treatise on powders, and if one cuts from the heart excessively, and it goes above, it will cause no harm;
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Treat it then, as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to the obstruction by stones, or frozen blood, or feces, or dead flesh, or similar things that we have mentioned in the section;
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	and if the urine is not released, and you see that the retention is due to a stone in the neck or at the mouth of the bladder, then it is necessary for the patient to be bent over their knees;
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	and let his feet be placed on his back, and stretch his belly from the part above the back, and restrain the patient as tightly as possible;
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	and then the neck of the bladder is forced for the expression of the stone above, which loosens the urine;
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer extraction with all the instrument which is called "catheter", of which this is the form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	and let it be of fine light silver, like the feathers of a bird;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and let the tube be one and a half palms long, and let it be fine at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the method of urine extraction is that you take a double thread, and tie at the head a ball of wool or cotton, and insert the end of the thread inside the urethra;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	and cut the excess wool and insert it to the end of the urethra, then anoint the urethra with oil or butter and egg white, and have the patient sit on a chair, and wet his bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and warm water;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	then gently insert the urethra into the penis until it reaches the base of the penis, then double the penis upwards towards the belly;
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	then push the urethra forward until it reaches the bladder, and the patient will feel it reach the empty space, and this is not done forcefully according to this method because the conduit through which it goes is twisted;
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	then the thread is applied to all the wool little by little, and the urine follows the wool, then extract it forcefully, and make the urine flow;
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and repeat the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When blood comes into the bladder, or corruption is gathered there, and you see aqueous and medicinal substances being distilled into it, then make use of all the instrument called "clepsydre," and this is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed, and has three openings:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	two on one side, and one on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the end is made such that the medicine is suitable to plug the penis well without addition, so that one may draw out moisture and insert when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you want to insert your medicine into the bladder, put the head of the container in the moisture, and draw with the syringe that is inside;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	so you will draw out the moisture with a scraper, and then firmly reattach by drawing inward;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	so the moisture will enter inside, and it will reach the bladder now, so that the patient will feel it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is the form of the subtle clyster with which one performs an enema on the bladder:
si est ci:	it is as follows:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is made of silver or bronze, and the head is higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and below the breast where the limb lies;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	then take a sheep's bladder and put the moisture in it with which you wish to perform the enema on the bladder, then tie it between the two breasts tightly with a strong doubled thread, and heat that moisture over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	then insert the head of the clyster into the penis, then draw your hand over the bladder as all the moisture comes in, until the patient feels that this moisture has just come to the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you do not have the bladder, then take a piece of parchment, and make a circle, and pierce it roundly around;
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then insert a strong thread into these holes, then close the circle as one closes a lid, and put inside what you wish of oil and moisture and water, and tie it to the instrument;
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do as you have done with the bladder, pressing with your hand until the moisture comes to the bladder.
de la piere	about the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have said before in the division the ways of stones, and the extraction together with medicine;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and I have said the difference between the stone in the reins, and all the signs, and in what kind of stone one should operate with cutting;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone which forms in the bladder occurs more often in children, and the sign is that the urine jumps from the bladder resembling pure urine in its fineness;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and there appears sand, and it irritates the patient's penis, and it can happen many times, and then it constricts;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and often these foundations shift;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the healing of children is quick until they are four years old, and it is very difficult in the elderly, and it is moderate for young adults, for those who are between youth and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	and the treatment is easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient with a cathartic, to draw out all the bile that is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes hinders seeking the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet, and lift him up and move him downward so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it leaves its higher position;
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then make him sit between your spread hands, and his hands should be below his thighs, so that the bladder is completely inclined downward;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then seek it and touch inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	if you feel the stone in the space, then hurry now to cut into the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not fall at the full touch, then moisten your index finger with oil from the left hand, if the patient is an adult, or your middle finger, if the patient is a fully grown youth;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and insert it into his anus, and seek the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, then pull it towards the neck of the bladder;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press with your finger, and push it out where you wish to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instructs the servant to press the bladder with his hand, and commands him to extend his right hand upwards towards the testicles, and with his left hand lift the skin that is beneath the testicles in the area where the belt is fastened;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	then he inserts the catheter cutting, which is of this form:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And make an incision between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but to the side of the left thigh;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and be straight on the stone, and your hands should be near the anus, and the incision should be wide at the top according to the size of the stone, and narrow inside, according to the quantity of the stone, not too large;
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	by chance the pressure on the tooth which is in the foundation, that it jumps out without effort;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and know that there is such a stone in which it has angles, and edges:
si est griés a issir;	it is difficult to remove;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and there is such one that is smooth, resembling an acorn, and round, from which the extraction is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	For those that have angles and edges, make the cut larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not jump out, then you must grasp with tongs that are like a file at the head, to grip the stone so that it does not escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	where you place under the eye a delicate curved instrument at the tip;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot manipulate it thus, then widen the small hole, and if the sinew is dry, then tighten it with vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there is more than one stone, then place the largest one first at the neck of the bladder, then cut above it, then pull it out forcefully, and the smaller ones after if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then you must saw it and make a larger incision.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	either he dies, or the urine comes immediately through the opening that the incision cannot close;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but nevertheless exert yourself in pulling it out, or in breaking it with forceps, until you pull it out in pieces;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and when you have completed your work, then dress the wound with incense and aloes and dragon's blood, and bind it, and put over it a cloth moistened in oil and wine, or in oil and rose water and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	then have the patient rest on their back, and do not loosen the binding until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you dislocate it, wash the area very well with oil and water, then treat it with ointment diaphoretic and basilicon ointment, until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	and if hot abscesses and corruptions, and clots of blood in the bladder come to the wound, and the urine is retained in such a way that it is formed without passing with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	then put your finger in the wound, and extract that blood, for if it remains, it will corrupt the bladder, and cause putrefaction;
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then raise the wound with water and ash and salt, and aid it in every way that you know, until it is healed;
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	and it is necessary that every time you treat it, you bind the two thighs, and apply the medicines to the site.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small and it is in the urethra of the penis, embedded inside, and the urine cannot pass;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	then treat it as I said before, that you cut it multiple times, and one is relieved by this treatment through cutting.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already proved it thus.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	Take an iron bar according to this form and let it have three pointed ends fixed in one piece.
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone so that it cannot move back into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	then insert the drill into the shaft gently, until it reaches the bone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and turn the drill with your hand in the bone little by little, until you can pierce through the other side of the bone;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	the urine will come soon, then press your hand on what remains of the bone that is inside the shaft.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	It will break soon, and it will come out with the urine, and the patient will be healed;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	and if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, then tie a thread below the bone and another above, then cut the shaft where the bone is between the two ties, then extract it forcefully, and untie the thread, and clean the congealed blood in the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of the stone of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	It sometimes happens that a stone is lodged in women, and if it ever happens, the treatment is difficult, and is forbidden for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second is that one cannot find a woman who is well-informed and exposes herself to midwives, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third reason is that perhaps one cannot find a woman who is well-skilled in this art with her hands;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	and the fourth reason is that the stone in the woman is more embedded than the stone in the man, which requires a deeper incision, and there is great fear. And if necessity demands this, then you must take a skilled midwife, who is hardly found, and if you do not find one, seek out a clever chaste midwife;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and presents a wise midwife in the lives of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and commands her to do what you command her for the examination of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and look very carefully if the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then he must insert his finger into the fundament and seek the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, she should press it beneath her finger, and she is advised to insert her finger into the patient's vagina, and to grasp and press firmly with her left hand on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, then she must move it gradually from the entrance of the bladder downward until it reaches the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	then cut into the stone at the root of the thigh opposite the middle of the groin, where it is pressed together, and feel the stone in that part;
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move his hand above or below the stone, and let the cut be small at first;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then insert the probe into the cut, if you feel the stone increase the wound until the stone can come out easily, and know that there are many kinds of stones:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	that is to say, small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and those that have edges.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	and know the similarities to understand the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and if the pain overcomes you, put ground vitriol at the site and keep it there for an hour until the pain subsides;
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	then return to your work, until the stone is strong, and have the instruments that I have told you in the extraction of the stone from men to help you in your work;
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	and if the blood overcomes you, and it is from the artery that is cut, then put the powder on the place and bind with cloths and bandages, and do not begin this again, and leave the stone and do not extract it, lest by chance the patient might die;
puis cure la plaie.	then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood is calmed, and the limb becomes strong, return to your work, until the stone is removed.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Aquous ramus is nothing other than an assembly of moisture or white substance, which is beneath the cover of the testicles, that contains the egg;
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and it is called “syfac”, and sometimes it is properly in the web of the eye, if one thinks that it is another egg;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and it is the skin of the groin between the white syfac that we have mentioned;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	and this does not happen if there is no pus.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this ramice is due to the weakness that comes to the testicles, and that material is spread out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the groin, and this moisture has many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	or it is a color tending to yellow, or it is without red, or black, or white watery, and this happens more often;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this assembly, for if it is in the white syfac that we have mentioned, then the abscess is hard, the pus long like the shape of an egg, and the groin does not appear, for it has moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if it has moisture in the inner fabric, then the abscess is hard with part of the yolk, and because of this people think it is another egg;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white surface, then it can be felt well;
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	then when you wish to know the color of the moisture, test all the inserted area carefully, of which the form is described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to what comes after the introduction, judge of what is within.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we cure it with iron, then it is necessary that the patient be bled according to our ability and the fullness of his body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then place him on his back, on something quite high, and put under him many cloths;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	then sit on his left, and instruct the assistant to sit on the right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs of the heart of the testicles;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	then take the sharp knife, and cut the skin of the testicles from the long part down to near the wrist, and let your incision be straight, dividing the skin of the testicles until the white surface, and peel it carefully according to your ability;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	then pierce the surface full of water with a wide hole, and draw out all the water, and then place your fingers, and stretch the surface upwards;
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the heart of the testicles, but only the surface;
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	cut it all or piece by piece especially the subtle part of it, that if you do not cut it wisely, the ailment will return;
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	and if the eye jumps during your work, reset it in its place when you have completed the work on the surface;
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then sew the two sides of the scrotum together with one stitch, then treat it like other wounds until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	and if you find the eye corrupted by another disease, then you must tie the vessels that are suspensory, out of fear of blood flow;
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	then cut the testicle at the suspensory ligament, and remove the eye, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if the fluid is gathered in two parts together, know that these are two branches;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	cut the other part as you have done the first equally, then wipe the blood, and put in the wound wool moistened in rose oil;
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and put over it more wool moistened in wine and oil, and place on the two groins, and put over that doubled cloths, and bind it tightly according to this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two cloths, and apply shredded wool according to this appearance and have them sewn together at the waistband of the breeches, and one of the shoulders should extend from the anus to the back, and the other to the part of the groin;
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and the other two heads on the two angles, and let the entire constriction be gathered into the loop of the strap;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and sometimes this branch of cautery is used instead of iron branding, and it is that you take a subtle knife-like cautery, and cut the skin of the testicles, and heat it as we have said, so that the white surface containing the fluid is exposed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	so take the cautery according to this form, and pierce that surface with tongs, and scrape it with this hot subtle cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	and cut it in every way that you can, until you clean everything;
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and be careful that the fire does not touch the egg;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this work is more healing;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and watchful of the flow of blood, and skilled in the works of circumcision;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if anything opposes you, whether an inflamed abscess or a flow of blood or something else, then treat what opposes you according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is fearful and does not wish to undergo this work because of its horror, then use perforation, as I tell you, and it is that when you are certain by the signs we have mentioned that watery phlegm is present, then make the patient sit on the elevated seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	then pierce the abscess in the part below all the swelling width, and apply the perforation from the long of the body;
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	and let the pores be wide, so that all the water flows through;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then put cotton on the area, and bind it, and leave it to drain the remaining water, then clean it until the wound is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	and if the white cloth does not allow water to come out of the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a quill or the instrument used to draw water from dropsical patients, the form of which is described above;
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and widen the wound little by little, and know that the water returns and gathers after about six months or so, and when it has gathered as before, thus will the patient spend his days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the section of this branch there is fear in many positions, which is why it seems better to leave it alone;
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the work and the similarities of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say then that many abscesses come to the body, especially to the testicles;
et c’est par mout de cas.	and it is by much chance.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	It is to be known by an excess of sour and watery humors, which spreads to the testicles, or from trauma;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	and the color of the abscess is according to the color of the body;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and finds no pain, and it is a severe abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and by chance some abscesses are severe and fearful and stony, and of a fox's color, and sometimes come from artery pus, or swelling of the vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from artery pus, it is known by the condition of the abscess being hot when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and you should not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	The one caused by swelling of the vein is known by its condition upon touching with the fingers, and one can properly perform the incision on this appearance, and on other parts;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and it is that you cut the core of the testicles, then the egg rises up, and the thread from the white surface, and free the suspensory ligament from all sides of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	if the egg is already cooked with these new veins, then you must draw out the egg and cut it;
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	and if it is airy on the surface, or in what is inside the vessels, then you must free all of that tissue, and cut it roundly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the flesh is at the rear place, then you must cut it all off and extract the egg, just as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your works are completed, then apply the wound with wool moistened in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess wrapped in a covering similar to a boil, with the softening of the testicles, and the patient suffers greatly when urinating;
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	and the treatment of this disease is as frightening as the one mentioned before, and nevertheless we will tell you its procedure according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	You must make the patient sit on the raised chair, then place the suspensory of the scrotum down with your hands, over the vessels that are close to the penis, and grasp the main ones, and stretch them firmly;
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	then cut with a broad sharp knife across the vessels until they are exposed, and then peel on each side, just as we have said in the extraction of the arteries in the temples;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	then insert a needle with double thread, and tie it at the first place where the vein emerged, and tie it again at the other end;
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	then cut them straight through the middle, according to the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted moisture;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	then treat the wound like the others where we cauterize blood, so that no vessel leaks which nourishes one of the testicles;
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	for by this no harm comes, and if pus comes to all the vessels, then it is necessary to draw the testicles from all the vessels;
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the organ does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and they dry out and cannot help each other.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the rupture of the spleen
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The effects of this procedure are by the section that comes to the groin, or the extension on the belly in the area of the thighs, so that the intestines descend from that rupture to one of the testicles;
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this rupture is at the level of the thigh or from the stretching of it, and these two types come from many causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	or from impact, or from jumping, or from crying, or from lifting heavy loads, and by similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs when it is from the stretching of the thigh, are that it happens little by little, over a long time, and does not come suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are equal up to the point of perfection, because the thigh presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the sign is when it is from the rupture of the spleen, that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and the swellings appear varied under the skin nearby, and this is due to the protrusion of the intestines and the body beyond the spleen.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the hernias come with the intestines, and are held there, causing great pain to the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron treatments there is fear, therefore one must avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of the work is that you instruct the patient to keep the intestines in place with their hand inside the wound, if they can reach in;
