puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then remember on his neck. between your hands, and lift the thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then bring the heart upward, and cut all the skin of the scrotum lengthwise;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then insert into the edges of the wound hooks according to what you need to open the wound, and they should be such that the pus may come out;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then peel the surface that is under the skin of the scrotum until the white hard surface is exposed on all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	then insert your index finger into what follows the testicle, between the white surface that is under the skin of the egg, and the second surface, and separate what is behind the egg, and between the second surface;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and then move the right hand inside the core of the testicles, and stretch the white part upwards with your left hand, and lift the eye to all the surface towards the waist;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the minister to stretch the eye upwards, and loosen that which is air behind the bandage;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and feel with your hands if there is any intestine wrapped around the hard white surface, and if you find anything, put it back into the abdomen;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take a needle on which there is thick thread made of several threads, and insert it into the back part of the surface, which is behind the skin of the testicles;
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	After the cutting, then cut the shoulders that appear from the threads, until there are four threads;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	then gather them one upon the other in the shape of a cross, and tie the superficie, which we have mentioned that is under the skin of the scrotum, with a strong binding of two parts;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then wrap the shoulders of the threads, and tie them firmly with two parts, so that none of the vessels that nourish them can enter within, to prevent a hot abscess from forming;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and place the binding according to the first binding long two times of that one, and after these two bindings leave from the superficie which is under the skin of the scrotum the length of one thumb;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and after all the other according to the roundness that the eye bears;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then cut in the part that is below the skin of the testicles, as much as the sinew and the vein, just as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply moistened wool in oil, and place it on the wounds, and apply the bandage that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white surface that we have mentioned is cauterized after the incision, out of fear of blood flowing.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this often happens, and leave the bandage until it falls off by itself;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it takes too long to fall off, let it be soaked in warm water, and put on what we have said until it falls off;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another treatment until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone who dared to perform the treatment with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is made like the twig which is together with the vine, in such a manner that you tie the vessels, after cutting lightly underneath;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then cut in the middle, and treat the abscess of the one who works until the vessels fall out;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes rupture occurs in the groin, as we have said, and the lump appears;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and none of the intestines should descend into the testicles, and if they do descend, it is bad, and recurs frequently;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and if it remains too long at this stage, the wound or abscess grows, so that the intestines descend;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens by the extension of the abscess which is in the veins, as we have said, for it is extended, then the blood is softened and swollen and opens;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the treatment is by cautery, as we have said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and sometimes it is treated with iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and it is that the patient lies down on his back between your hands, then cut the swollen area of the rupture according to the width of three fingers;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then extract the sebaceous substance that is under the skin which follows, then take the ointment and put it on the area where the sebaceous substance appears;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press it perfectly on the belly, then sew the two areas where the sebaceous substance appears at the head of the ointment, and sew one and the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then extract the head of the ointment, and do not cut into the sebaceous substance nor stretch the egg or any other thing, as I have made known to you in the treatment of the removal of the intestines;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	then treat it according to the treatment of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the abscesses, dress and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The suture is tight, and there is no appearance in the rupture, and the cauterization is milder in this area, and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	often the skin of the testicles in some men is softened because the semen inside is liquefied, and it is noticeable;
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	and it is necessary, when one wants to treat him, that the patient lie down on his back, and cut the skin which has softened on the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	then bring the two lips together with a suture, and if you see, first sew the excess of the softened skin with three or four firm sutures;
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	then cut between the sutures, and treat it like other wounds until it is healed, and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	from the chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that castrations are condemned in our law, and for this reason I would prefer not to speak of it in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is not necessary except for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	where one is that the physician should know how to answer when asked, and know the treatment;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, because we often need to use certain animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and other animals.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say then that castrations are performed in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either by attraction, or by incision.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the one that we do by attraction, we make the animal sit in hot water until the testicles are softened and hanging;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then take them in your hand until they are repositioned and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the chastisement of gout:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	you must dye the animal, and press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and cut on each egg with one cut, when you have thoroughly skinned them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave some of the fat from the intestines and the fine fat that is on the vessels;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this method of castration is better than that which is done by attraction, because in the attraction sometimes something of the testicles remains, by which the animal desires lust;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	about hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermafrodite exists according to two ways among humans:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one of which is that between the two testicles there appears as the figure of a woman's anatomy, where it has hair, and sometimes it passes urine through it.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And another manner is in women, and it is on the wrist like a rod and two eggs.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for the man and the woman is that you cut away all the attached flesh, and treat it like other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	in the second way, for men whose urine passes through the skin of the testicles, there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	of the tension
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tentigene is a piece of flesh attached to the natural part, such that it is too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have it as large as a hand, and that is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You must dye the excess of the tendons to your hand or with needles, and lightly cut it away;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not go too deep, so that bleeding does not occur, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed;
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and to another growth that appears at the mouth of the molar, and it spreads, and perhaps grows large, and resembles a cup, and for this reason the ancients called it "cup disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	So you must cut it off, as we have said about the tendon, and treat it until it is healed.
de erratique	The term "erratique" seems to be related to the English word "erratic," which generally means unpredictable, irregular, or deviating from what is usual or expected. However, since your query is brief and lacks context, I've provided a general translation. If you need more specific information or context about how it's used, please provide additional details.
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	It is erratic when the nature of the woman is not perceived, or the opening is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is caused by birth, or accidentally by disease that has come;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is by a car attached, or from the surface subtle or thick, and is done in perfection in the marrow, or on the sides, or below, or wherever it may be;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and defend the conception, and the childbirth, and perhaps the flows to have;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the knowledge of this is by the regard of the bile.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the swelling is closely appearing, then grasp it with your hands or with a cloth.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	if it is from the surface subtle, and it is close to the two temples, then you should hurry, and do it thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	put your two index fingers together, and the woman should be on her back, with her legs spread apart;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then stretch the two temples properly, until the subtle surface is rounded, and it covers the swelling;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool, and anoint it with oil, and place it on the area, and have the woman lie with the man each day so that it does not heal.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the surface is hard and thick, then you should scrape it with a spatula shaped like a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the swelling is from a new growth, then suspend it at the onset and cut it off;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have the blood-stopping medicines, such as acacia, dragon's blood, frankincense, all mixed with egg white;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	then apply a wide bandage to the wound so that it cannot heal closed;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and let it be for a long time, and apply a linen cloth to it;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat other treatments until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when new flesh comes in the wound, it must be cut according to this method, unless they are infected abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For an infected abscess that is in the wound, one should not touch it with iron.
des emorroides	hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that without cause usually occur, and when hemorrhoids are old they become hard.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and we have said before in the division the similarities of them, and the signs, and I will say here those that receive cure.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that the hemorrhoids and the withered parts, when they are perfect in the anus, and they do not appear to the touch, are not cured by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the mouth of the anus, which can be felt, are those that can be treated.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	Therefore, you must put the woman in a cold house, then stretch the altar with tongs, and cut it at its roots, then powder on blood-stopping medicines, such as agaric and dragon's blood and frankincense, and similar things;
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then place her feet to the wall for an hour, then put her in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if there is an overflow of blood, then have her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate peel and galls and similar things, and then take barley flour, and mix it with honey and salt, and make a plaster on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it is stopped, it is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	and if not, have leeches applied to the back and breasts without pricking;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take wool, and boil it in plantain juice or in elder juice with old wine, and apply it to the area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has subsided, treat the area with ointment until it is healed;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called "albathir" is red, and resembles a hard head, so it must be cut as I have said for the thelul;
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	of the abscesses of the jaw
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscesses occur in the jaw, such as ulcers and stony abscesses and herpes and aphthae and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscesses, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the classification.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It is then necessary that I speak in this treatise about the hot abscess that comes in the marrow, which is not one of the abscesses collected by the bow.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you wish to know the work of iron, then observe if the abscess is sharp at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and if it turns red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hurry to pierce it, but let it ripen until the pain is calmed;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then make the patient sit on a chair, and have two small stools where he can lean, and support his back and bring his feet together below the leg;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and let his thighs be spread apart, and place his arms beneath his knees, and bind them well with a good binding;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	then the servant turns it towards the right side, and applies the instrument with which one works the mouth of the maris, from which comes the form;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you apply this instrument, you first insert the rod to know the depth of the maris, so that what enters inside the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and it does not injure the patient;
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the maris with cloths, so that the instrument does not cause pain;
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and it is necessary that he place the cone of the instrument above, and that he stain the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	and when the abscess is opened, and one cuts it with a soft hand, then it must be cut at the top, with the spatula lightly;
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the boil is emptied, then you must put into the wound cloths moistened in rose oil, or in dried green oil;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and place the cloth firmly on the wound at the center of the poultice, and put over the poultice and on the bandage clean wool moistened in water or in which mallows have been cooked;
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat it after two days of anointing in this manner, until it is healed;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and sometimes lift the wound and the sore by aclyster of water and honey, and then with water or roots of lilies and long fennel being cooked;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to the ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is embedded in the flesh, then you must beware of using hot iron, but treat it as we have said in the section.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary first for the midwife to know the signs of natural childbirth, and these signs are when you see the woman pressing downwards, and desiring to smell the air.
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the infant hastens to come out;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then you know that this childbirth is according to the natural form, and the exit is under its head, and the afterbirth with it;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, then it is necessary to lightly press his belly, so that the infant comes out quickly;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when he urinates on his head, the afterbirth comes with it, and the mother is cleansed of her excesses through proper cleansing;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and he who comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For sometimes he comes on his feet, and the body or the shoulders, and the hands come forward, or he comes on his belly, or his buttocks, and is turned by chance on his neck, and in other bad positions;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and skilled in these matters, and to beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the positions how one should assist them.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the fetus comes onto its head by natural passage, and the woman gives birth with difficulty, and the strength of the woman is weak, then have her sit on a saddle, where the women hold her;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and her natural oils or fenugreek be cooked, and then the midwife puts between her fingers the small spatula of which this is the form:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and cut through the amnion, and scrape with her nail until the moisture inside comes out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and grasp the woman's belly until the fetus descends, and if it does not descend, then it is necessary to administer an enema to the woman with a mixture of fenugreek and sesame oil;
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then have her sneeze from condiments, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	the infants will now come out.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if the two hands come out forcefully, then you must reset them gently little by little;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot go in, then put the woman on a stool and lift her feet up;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then place the stool on the ground, and support the woman so she does not fall when it is lowered;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hand cannot enter and the infant is dead, then cut the hands with the knife that was previously placed there, extract the infant, and reset equally.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of the birth of the child on its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the infant comes on its feet, then he must be pushed up;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little until it is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then take the feet and stretch them little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When it reaches up to the thighs, then command to take hold of it, and make it sneeze with condiments;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if it is strong, if God wills.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not become strong as we have said, then turn it little by little until it is according to the natural shape.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it moves lightly.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come strong as we have, say take musliage of altitude, and oil of sesame, and dissolved gum, and grind all in the mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and put on the nature of the woman inside and remove this ointment, then have her sit in warm water up to below the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is moistened underneath, make her a necklace of myrrh, and put it underneath, and leave it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on the seat, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and gently grasp her belly, for the infant is now jumping.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the birth of the child upon its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the infant comes in this manner, then the midwife gradually places her hands;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then let it be held by its neck, and its feet dangled down, and let it lie on the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and bends his hands little by little, and then takes hold of the hands on the belly, and removes the cushions underneath, until she is aligned downwards;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the infant does not jump, then take its feet and move them forcefully, then move its belly upwards, then put your hands there;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and wash the child little by little;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and command the woman to strain until the infant comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the birth of the child who comes with one hand extended wide
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary to devise a way to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if it cannot be brought back, then make the woman stand up and walk;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If she cannot walk, then make her lie on the bed, and raise her legs properly;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then administer the massage that I have described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, then make her sit on the stool, then try to guide the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and take the child according to its natural position, and make her sneeze, and command her to strain until the infant comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	from the birth of the child on its neck, and have its hands spread out, and its face turned towards its mother's back.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	it is necessary that the bailiff hold his hand, then turn it little by little, and take it gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is aligned, then apply the natural massage with fat and oil, as we have said, then command her to move little by little;

et la fai esternuer.	and make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in this same manner to all the secondine
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes to this manner of fullness in the sinew, cut the sinew with your nail until the moisture is emptied;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the swelling can be on his face and neck, then cut it from the boil so that it is not retained, and reduce the swelling;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then place the child inside, until you have put it in the proper position, and command the woman to hold herself firmly;
adonques si istra legierement.	then it will come out easily.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the birth of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that abscesses often occur, and sometimes three or four may develop;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not an unusual thing, and it often happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two are unusual things, and they do not live much, if at all;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they multiply, and are separated by the surface that divides them, which is tied to the knot;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they come out as naturally as any other bodily fluids, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they come out forcefully, then treat it as we have said, and let the bandage be fine, and do quickly and lightly what needs to be done;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do so as it moves to salvation.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the womb I or II or III or IIII or V or VI or VII, or more up to XV, and are all shaped like children by the measurement of the wise glorious, and it is necessary that the midwife knows all this, for perhaps similar things happen to her;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	and do according to what is appropriate.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat the woman for a dead child in her womb, as I have said in the division, and it does not come out, and you are constrained to manual work;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	you must know if the woman is of sound health, and has no condition where she fears death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	so that the woman must lie on her back, and have her hips inclined downward, and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the minister holds the thread in two parts, tied to the bed so that it is not pulled during the descent of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth of the mother with moist oils mixed with alum and fenugreek and flaxseed, then anoint her hands with these oils and these mixtures;

et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and it is necessary that he holds the needle in his right hand, and places the ball between the fingers of his left hand, and gently applies it to his entire hand, and inserts the needle into any of these areas that we have mentioned until it reaches the empty space;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the form of the needle:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then insert another needle opposite it, or a third if needed, so that the extractions are equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then stretch it evenly by moving from one side to the other, to make the teeth come out, and let the bone be toothed to hold the teeth, as is shown here:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	and if part of it remains, he anoints one of his fingers with oil, and puts it in that part, and pulls the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if any remains, place this bone at the higher part, and do this until it all comes out completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	and if one hand comes in front of the other and cannot be brought back due to constriction, then you must wrap it with a cloth until it all comes out;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	then cut at the joint of the sole or at the toe, and thus you must do in the other hand, and to the two feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the shoulder of the child is large and it is stuck in the birth canal, or it has a pointed head gathered together, then you must put the sharp spathouse between your fingers, cut the head and draw out the water;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you round it with the instrument which is called "almidach," from which the form comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and in the same way do it if the infant has a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull the bones with tongs, and if the shoulder is tight inside and it resists with strength, it should be split until the moisture which is in the swelling comes out;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if she cannot come out, then cut her into pieces with the tool you can use;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or below the ribs, then you must pierce it until the moisture flows.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on his feet, then the attraction is light, and the adjustment to the mouth of the wound is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is tight in the belly or the breast, then you must stretch it with a cloth wrapped around the hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and cut open the belly or the breast until the moisture that is inside flows;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other limbs are removed and the head remains, then the healer puts his hand into the fontanel of the skull, and pulls it until the mouth of the skull;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then place one lancet or two, and draw forcefully;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the opening of the ear is narrowed due to a hot abscess that has come there, one should not work on it, but instead administer moist and greasy substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the treatment should be plasters, and sitz baths in softening and moistening water.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the infant is on its side, and you can make it lie flat, then administer what we have said for the living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one cannot do so, then draw forcefully piece by piece, and leave nothing of the second skin.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if the attendant removes what we have said about hot abscesses that come in the groin;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding occurs, then apply constricting water, and the attendant should perform other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose womb one fetus had been dead, then another was placed on top of it, and the other also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came upon the boil, and swelled so much that it burst open, and began to have great pus.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat, and I thought long about it, and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I put on a strongly attracting poultice, and an bone came out, and after some days others did as well.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very amazed, because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I stitched the wound, and pulled out many bones, until the woman was in better condition;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman lived for a long time this way, and would occasionally discharge a bit of pus from the site;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have recalled this chapter for the reason that when a master finds something unusual, he should add help to it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring back the dislocated to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Here comes the form of the compressor, to which one lifts the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and to two wheels at the two shoulders of the two limbs.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horn should be finer than the restrictive part, and it should be made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the staff should be one inch wide, and the margin of the branches one inch, and in length one and a half palms;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between the two limbs should be two adjustments of this same staff, which are fixed at one end and the other, half a palm in length or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two adjustments are inserted into the mouth of the marrow to open when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, should be made of ebony wood or boxwood, according to the shape of the forceps;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and let it have at both ends two adjustments, as you see, one palm long, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you wish to open the uterus with the entire instrument, make the woman sit on a bed, feet hanging and legs spread, then insert the two adjustments together into the uterus, and hold the head of the instrument below between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand with the entire instrument, just as you have done with the forceps equally, according to the amount that you wish to open the mouth of the uterus, until the loose part does what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all coated, and their appearances are multiplied;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	and when the doctor has prepared them, he is more eager to work, and they are more valuable to people because of their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despair of the instrument that you have prepared, for their necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold back her flow, and then make her sneeze with condice, and hold her hands to her mouth and neck;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she succeeds by this means, it is good.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, then take a pot, and make holes in the lid, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the womb inside, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia lignea, and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all these herbs, or some of them, be cooked in a pot with water over the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then put one end of a cane or tube into the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the patient, and have them inhale until the vapor comes inside the patient;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make them sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	The sinews move swiftly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if it remains after this treatment and does not come out, then instruct the nurse to moisten her left hand in sesame oil or in a mixture of altitude, and then place it on the area, and rub gently;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, then grasp it and extend it little by little straightly, so that the patient does not fall during the extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but there it is necessary to move lightly to the right and to the left, and then pull;
si venra et se desaerdra.	it will come and dislocate.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the opening of the ear is too narrow, we have mentioned the treatment of sneezing and the fumigation of herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it does not go through all of what we have said, be careful that you do not follow in pulling;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that what is at the opening of the ear be tied to the thigh of the woman, then cleanse it with an ointment of four drugs;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	it will swell and reset, and come back strong;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but nonetheless, when it ferments, a bad odor comes to the stomach and head, and hurts the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	then appropriate fumigations are needed for this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	some of the ancients have experienced fumigations of watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman for the retention of the flows and the secondina is thus:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it resembles glass, with a thin head placed in the affected area, and the wide ends over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigation be over the coals, and continue until it is consumed, and start another one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the anus
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have a perforated anus, but it is plugged with a thin membrane:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	then it is necessary for the nurse that she pierces that surface appropriately, and does not pierce it with an acute spatula, and takes care of the stitching so as not to touch it;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then put wet wool in wine and oil, then the treatment of anointing until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not heal, put a pin of silver in the puncture and leave it for several days, and remove it when the child wishes to go into chambers.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this swelling comes from the suddenness of a wound or an abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	then it is necessary to cut that sudden swelling:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	it should be treated, as we have said about the splinter.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula of the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from beneath the anus are nodulations, and enlargements that come near the anus or in the space between the two parts, so there is one fistula or more;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when that knotting is old, it acts, and still moisture causes white or subtle sores, and sometimes these fistulas are perforating;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and they are known by what comes out in excretion or flatulence when the patient excretes, and sometimes one jumps out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And there are fistulas that penetrate as far as the bladder, and up to half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and they extend as far as the hip joint, and up to the knee pit.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the perforating fistula at the anus, and the non-perforating:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and it is that you put your index finger in the anus, and insert a fine needle of brass or iron into the fistula when there is no tortuosity.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	and if there is tortuosity, then insert a thin lead probe or horsehair until you feel the probe or hair at its proper place;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no discharge of feces or wind or worm from the opening, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not penetrate;
si te haste dou curer.	do not hurry to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula extends all the way to the bladder or to the urinary duct, then the urine leaks out and cannot be sealed with medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	if it is penetrated up to the junction of the thigh, then the probe reaches the site;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no curvature and the source of the pain around it, then it immediately causes swelling, and neither medicine nor salve by ointment is effective;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these Persian fistulas there is no cure other than work, and the vanity of foolish doctors who interfere with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In the one that is not Persian and is not old, there is hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced, and it is that the patient lies between your hands on their back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and the legs are lifted up to his thighs, and his thighs are inclined toward his abdomen;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a probe of silver, or of bronze if there is curvature, until you know where the probe goes.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around the anus, then you must put your index finger there, and if you sense that the tent has pierced through;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and it is uncovered where you feel between your finger the surface or the flesh, then you know that it is pierced through;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	do not tamper with it, for it cannot be healed;
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said nonetheless that some can be healed well, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid that is done consists in heating the fine cautery according to the width of the fistula, as was previously stated;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and he inserts it entirely hot into the fistula until it comes near the anus;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two times or three, until you know that these charred remains are burned, which look like the feather of a bird;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then clean with moistened tents in butter, until the charred parts come out, then cleanse with an ointment that heals and binds the wound.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is thus healed, it is well.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this is done, no other healing can be achieved;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent enters and does not penetrate to the bone at the base, and between your finger and the tent there is a thick covering of char or scab, and you see the fistula beneath this covering of the wound;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	cut from the beginning of the fistula, and immediately push the tent further in, then cauterize afterward until you reach the head of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the tent shall be delivered, and fall;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then purify those stained charcoals that resemble a bird's feather, and leave nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the sinew overpowers you and cuts between you and the work, then cauterize it with fire or medicinal heat.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cauterization brings together two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the binding of these charcoals applied, and the stopping of blood and the drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then treat the moist tents with butter or ground substances until the place throws out pus, and let the burned charcoals be expelled in the pus;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound with sudorific ointments that soften hard flesh, and these medicines are dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes up to the perfect part of the anus and is away from the body, put your finger in the anus and probe it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tension, and between two is the thread or the sinew or flesh, where it is close to piercing, there is no force but the way of faith and hope, by the administration of one of the three ways:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it to the bottom, or if you can, place threads and treat it as first mentioned;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep that you do not cut the tissue holding the foundation, and excretions come out involuntarily;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	perchance it will be healed, or you remove that covering and clean it after it is cut near the foundation, whether by thread or by another sharpened instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then cleanse that dirty flesh which is in the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	then study to restore the wound, and to keep the fistula in the part outside the anus:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	it is a lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes the fistulas are according to this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and it is when you insert the tent into the fistula, and it is on the side of the anus near the skin above, then take a tent pierced at the top according to this form:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And you put the twisted thread in two, and insert the tent with all the thread into the fistula until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	if it is passing through the margin of the anus inside, then pull the thread from that hole, as you insert your finger into the anus;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and pull the head of the thread, and bring the two shoulders together, and press one against the other, and leave it for one day or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it sometimes until the thread cuts these tissues that are between two and fall out;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed and sealed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not drain, then have it pierced in every way you can, if it is not too hard.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not right to cut so hard for the lancing, and then clean it, as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the sharp spatumile spine, with which one makes the fistula, is very sharp on one side and cutting;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other side it is not, so that one does not cut what should not be cut, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Emorrhoids are according to two manners:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	where they are inside the fundament, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and they bring immediate blood, and if there is one or more, and they are below the fundament and at the top of the fundament;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those that are below have little moisture, and still bring a bit of yellow water or a bit of blood, and they have the color of the flesh;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have them inside the fundament is that you instruct the patient to strain to go into chambers, until the fundament comes out, and the threads become visible;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	then you hurry and grasp it with tweezers, or hold it with your nail, then cut it at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the forceps cannot hold them due to their moisture, then they take them with a flag, or with cotton, or with a piece of camlet;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and pull them out with your fingers, then cut them, and sprinkle some hot powders used for cautery on top;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cautery, then treat them with other treatments until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the fundament cannot expel [the matter], then purge the patient with a sharp and harshclyster to wash what is in the fundament so that it may be expelled easily;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	when the patient purges, and if the contents are strong from the fundament, then the treatment is light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and it is that you take them with your nail or with tongs, and cut them, then clean them as we have said, until they are healed, and the incision by iron is feared.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	and you must treat the stitch according to this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	take the twisted thread, and put it in a needle, and then pull the thread above and make the needle pierce from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle, and let it be wide;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and tighten the thread firmly, then knot the thread, and remove the needle, and do this for all the others, and leave one to draw off the excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then put on the fundament a moist cloth in rose oil or in ointment, and put it on the fundament, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave it until they defecate, and when they have done so, treat them with ointment and other treatments, until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from the dryness of the feces or wound
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often it happens that dryness of phlegm occurs in the intestines, and by constraint of nature, and when the disease is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	You must use the tip of a spatula or your nail to remove the outer layer that should not be allowed to become damp;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then treat it until it is properly cleansed as appropriate;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it does not heal, then repeat the shaving more forcefully than before, until it heals well and is peeled;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat until it is healed.
dou fremit	from the trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Formice is a small spotted appearance around the body, and it causes much harm;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes the cold affects it, and it is felt like a numbness from trembling, and it comes over the whole body, more so in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a quill from a goose feather, or a strong vulture feather, and place that quill on the trembling, until the circle fully encircles the trembling;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then turn your hand around the quill until you cut all around the trembling, and it stops the harm, and removes the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you wish, do this with a quill of brass or iron according to this form, and let it be sharp below and broad above.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	and does not perceive, to keep the eye still, and to press on it.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you wish, cauterize the tremor, as it is described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	about the form of the clyster
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes a clyster is made of silver or archaut, or of melted tin or lead;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and sometimes these substances are made small and large, according to those to whom they are administered.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those that are administered in the treatment of children and those who are weak and painful, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the clyster, whether small or large, is wide at the top, where the belly is tied according to this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	and there should be an opening where the belly is tied, as you see, and the inside of the cheeks be pierced;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and it should have two holes on one side, and one hole on the other;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and let the belly where one puts the medicines be of a beast's bladder or of parchment, and be pierced all around with small holes, and have between each hole one inch of space, then put in these holes one strong thread of raw silk twisted ten times around, and gather the belly so that it is like a bag;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	and when the medicine is inside, tie the instrument tightly with a strong thread, then use as an enema;
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is the form of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	and let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the enema with oil or egg white, or a similar thing, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	then the minister heats it with his two hands together until it is all hot, then draws out theclyster, and lifts the patient’s legs to the wall, and if the medicine wants to come out, holds it as much as he can;
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if he sleeps all night, it is greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you clysterize in a disease of diarrhea, and the medicine rushes to come out, restart it until it is absorbed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	and if the hemorrhoids are in the anus or an abscess, then let theclyster be as mild as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the mildclyster with which the skin should be drawn tight:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have said before in the section about the treatment of wounds;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	Or we shall tell you of the treatments of hands and medicine, according to the fulfillment.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made by, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and of what they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are by throwing of stones, and cutting of sword and knife, or spear or staff or arrow, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or they are made according to the parts of the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, or on the head, or the chest, or the belly, or the liver, and similar members;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, for the reminiscence will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head, and the bone is not broken, then take care if it is from throwing of stones or similar things, and the skin is entirely ruptured and the wound is large, and you fear the rising of a hot abscess:
